<DESCRIPTION>EXHIBIT 99.1

<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>Exhibit 99.1</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>[EXECUTION COPY] </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>LIMITED WAIVER, AMENDMENT AND RETENTION OF RIGHTS 
</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ACKNOWLEDGMENT AGREEMENT </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>THIS AGREEMENT </B>is dated as of August&nbsp;15, 
2014 between Penn West Petroleum Ltd. (the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;) and each
noteholder (each a &#147;<B>Noteholder</B>&#148; and, collectively, the 
&#147;<B>Noteholders</B>&#148;) under the Note Purchase Agreement dated 
May&nbsp;31, 2007 among the Company and the Purchasers listed in Schedule A 
attached thereto as holders
of the outstanding senior guaranteed notes of the Company issued thereunder (as 
amended, restated, supplemented or otherwise modified from time to time, the 
&#147;<B>Note Agreement</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B><U>PREAMBLE</U></B>: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">A. 
Capitalized terms
used in this Agreement without express definition shall have the same meanings 
as are ascribed to such terms in the Note Agreement and section references 
herein are to sections of the Note Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">B. The Company has issued a press release on 
July&nbsp;29, 2014 (the &#147;<B>Press Release</B>&#148;) announcing that the 
Audit Committee of
the Company&#146;s Board of Directors is conducting a voluntary internal review 
of certain of its accounting practices and that the Board of Directors of the 
Company has concluded that certain of the Company&#146;s historical financial 
statements
for the 2012 and 2013 fiscal years of the Company and the quarterly financial 
statements for its first fiscal quarter of 2014 (the &#147;<B>Relevant 
Periods</B>&#148;) must be restated (the &#147;<B>Restatement 
Decision</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">C. The Company has delivered a notice to each 
Noteholder under Section&nbsp;7.1(d) advising that as a result of the 
Restatement Decision, the
Company is in Default under: (a)&nbsp;Sections 7.1(a) and 7.1(b) (as they relate
to the statement that the financial statements be prepared in accordance with 
GAAP) (the &#147;<B>Financial Reporting Default</B>&#148;), and
(b)&nbsp;Section&nbsp;9.6
in respect of the requirement of the Company to maintain books and records of 
account in accordance with GAAP (the &#147;<B>Covenant Default</B>&#148;, and 
together with the Financial Reporting Default, the &#147;<B>Specified 
Defaults</B>&#148;).
Under the terms of Section&nbsp;11, each Specified Default has a cure period of 
30 days after a Responsible Officer obtains actual knowledge of such default 
(the &#147;<B>Cure Period</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">D. The Company&#146;s ongoing internal review in 
connection with the Restatement Decision may include the review of financial 
statements
prepared for periods prior to the Relevant Periods (&#147;<B>Pre-Relevant Period
Financial Statements</B>&#148;) that may result in the Company becoming aware of
Defaults or Events of Default under (a)&nbsp;Sections 5.5, 7.1(a) and 7.1(b) (as
they
relate to the requirement that such Pre-Relevant Period Financial Statements be 
prepared in accordance with GAAP, and certifications to that effect in 
certificates of officers delivered pursuant to Section&nbsp;7.2), and 
(b)&nbsp;Section&nbsp;9.6 in
respect of the requirement of the Company to maintain books and records of 
account in accordance with GAAP (each, a &#147;<B>Pre-2012 Default</B>&#148; and
collectively with the Specified Defaults, the &#147;<B>Applicable 
Defaults</B>&#148;). </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="center">- 2 - </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">E. The Company is party to an amended and restated 
credit agreement dated May&nbsp;6, 2014 (the
&#147;<B>Credit Agreement</B>&#148;) between the Company, as borrower, the 
financial institutions and other persons party thereto as lenders (the 
&#147;<B>Lenders</B>&#148;) and Canadian Imperial Bank of Commerce, as agent of 
the Lenders (the
&#147;<B>Agent</B>&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">F. The accounting 
practices causing the Restatement Decision have resulted in one or more defaults
under the
Credit Agreement (each a &#147;<B>Restatement Decision Credit Agreement 
Default</B>&#148;) and each such default is subject to a cure period of 30 days 
after the giving of notice thereof by the Agent to the Company, or such later 
date as the Lenders
and the Agent may agree in accordance with the Credit Agreement (the 
&#147;<B>Credit Agreement Cure Period</B>&#148;). The Agent has provided such 
notice to the Company (the &#147;<B>Credit Agreement Default Notice</B>&#148;) 
and a copy of such
notice has been provided to each Noteholder<B><I>.</I></B> The Company, the 
Agent and the Lenders have entered into a limited waiver agreement (the 
&#147;<B>Bank Waiver Agreement</B>&#148;) in respect of the Restatement Decision
Credit Agreement
Default and a copy of the Bank Waiver Agreement has been provided to each 
Noteholder. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">G. The Company is a party to six 
other Note
Agreements (the &#147;<B>Other Note Agreements</B>&#148;) having terms 
substantially the same as the Note Agreement, and there exists, under each one, 
defaults that are substantially equivalent to the Applicable Defaults 
(&#147;<B>Restatement
Decision Other Note Agreement Defaults</B>&#148;), having a cure period 
substantially the same as the Cure Period (the &#147;<B>Other Note Agreement 
Cure Periods</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">H. In accordance with Section&nbsp;18.1, the 
agreements contained herein require the approval of the Required Holders. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">I. Subject to the terms and provisions hereof, the 
Company has requested that the Noteholders agree to a limited waiver of the Pre-
2012
Defaults, to extend the date by which quarterly financial statements are due for
the second fiscal quarter of 2014, to extend the Cure Period and to amend 
certain terms and provisions of the Note Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B><U>AGREEMENT</U></B>: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>NOW 
THEREFORE</B>
in consideration of the premises, the covenants and the agreements herein 
contained and for other good and valuable consideration, the receipt and 
sufficiency of which is hereby acknowledged between the parties, the parties 
agree as follows: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">The Noteholders agree to extend the Cure Period to the 
earliest of: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the earlier of: (i)&nbsp;October&nbsp;14, 2014, and 
(ii)&nbsp;the date by which the Company must under applicable Law deliver its 
quarterly
financial statements for the second fiscal quarter of 2014 (the 
&#147;<B>Extended Delivery Date</B>&#148;); </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P 
STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the earlier of (i)&nbsp;the last day of the Credit 
Agreement Cure Period or (ii)&nbsp;the Other Note Agreement Cure Periods; 
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.2 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>[EXECUTION COPY] </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>LIMITED WAIVER, AMENDMENT AND RETENTION OF RIGHTS 
</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ACKNOWLEDGMENT AGREEMENT </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>THIS AGREEMENT </B>is dated as of August&nbsp;15, 
2014 between Penn West Petroleum Ltd. (the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;) and each
noteholder (each a &#147;<B>Noteholder</B>&#148; and, collectively, the 
&#147;<B>Noteholders</B>&#148;) under the Note Purchase Agreement dated 
May&nbsp;29, 2008 among the Company and the Purchasers listed in Schedule A 
attached thereto as holders
of the outstanding senior guaranteed notes of the Company issued thereunder (as 
amended, restated, supplemented or otherwise modified from time to time, the 
&#147;<B>Note Agreement</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B><U>PREAMBLE</U></B>:<B> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" 
ALIGN="justify">A. Capitalized
terms used in this Agreement without express definition shall have the same 
meanings as are ascribed to such terms in the Note Agreement and section 
references herein are to sections of the Note Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">B. The Company has issued a press release on 
July&nbsp;29, 2014 (the &#147;<B>Press Release</B>&#148;) announcing that the 
Audit Committee of
the Company&#146;s Board of Directors is conducting a voluntary internal review 
of certain of its accounting practices and that the Board of Directors of the 
Company has concluded that certain of the Company&#146;s historical financial 
statements
for the 2012 and 2013 fiscal years of the Company and the quarterly financial 
statements for its first fiscal quarter of 2014 (the &#147;<B>Relevant 
Periods</B>&#148;) must be restated (the &#147;<B>Restatement
Decision</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">C. The Company has delivered a notice to each 
Noteholder under Section&nbsp;7.1(d) advising that as a result of the 
Restatement Decision, the
Company is in Default under: (a)&nbsp;Sections 7.1(a) and 7.1(b) (as they relate
to the statement that the financial statements be prepared in accordance with 
GAAP) (the &#147;<B>Financial Reporting Default</B>&#148;), and 
(b)&nbsp;Section&nbsp;9.6
in respect of the requirement of the Company to maintain books and records of 
account in accordance with GAAP (the &#147;<B>Covenant Default</B>&#148;, and 
together with the Financial Reporting Default, the &#147;<B>Specified 
Defaults</B>&#148;).
Under the terms of Section&nbsp;11, each Specified Default has a cure period of 
30 days after a Responsible Officer obtains actual knowledge of such default 
(the &#147;<B>Cure Period</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">D. The Company&#146;s ongoing internal review in 
connection with the Restatement Decision may include the review of financial 
statements
prepared for periods prior to the Relevant Periods (&#147;<B>Pre-Relevant Period
Financial Statements</B>&#148;) that may result in the Company becoming aware of
Defaults or Events of Default under (a)&nbsp;Sections 5.5, 7.1(a) and 7.1(b) (as
they
relate to the requirement that such Pre-Relevant Period Financial Statements be 
prepared in accordance with GAAP, and certifications to that effect in 
certificates of officers delivered pursuant to Section&nbsp;7.2), and 
(b)&nbsp;Section&nbsp;9.6 in
respect of the requirement of the Company to maintain books and records of 
account in accordance with GAAP (each, a &#147;<B>Pre-2012 Default</B>&#148; and
collectively with the Specified Defaults, the &#147;<B>Applicable 
Defaults</B>&#148;). </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="center">- 2 - </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">E. The Company is party to an amended and restated 
credit agreement dated May&nbsp;6, 2014 (the
&#147;<B>Credit Agreement</B>&#148;) between the Company, as borrower, the 
financial institutions and other persons party thereto as lenders (the 
&#147;<B>Lenders</B>&#148;) and Canadian Imperial Bank of Commerce, as agent of 
the Lenders (the
&#147;<B>Agent</B>&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">F. The accounting 
practices causing the Restatement Decision have resulted in one or more defaults
under the
Credit Agreement (each a &#147;<B>Restatement Decision Credit Agreement 
Default</B>&#148;) and each such default is subject to a cure period of 30 days 
after the giving of notice thereof by the Agent to the Company, or such later 
date as the Lenders
and the Agent may agree in accordance with the Credit Agreement (the 
&#147;<B>Credit Agreement Cure Period</B>&#148;). The Agent has provided such 
notice to the Company (the &#147;<B>Credit Agreement Default Notice</B>&#148;) 
and a copy of such
notice has been provided to each Noteholder<B><I>.</I></B> The Company, the 
Agent and the Lenders have entered into a limited waiver agreement (the 
&#147;<B>Bank Waiver Agreement</B>&#148;) in respect of the Restatement Decision
Credit Agreement
Default and a copy of the Bank Waiver Agreement has been provided to each 
Noteholder. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">G. The Company is a party to six 
other Note
Agreements (the &#147;<B>Other Note Agreements</B>&#148;) having terms 
substantially the same as the Note Agreement, and there exists, under each one, 
defaults that are substantially equivalent to the Applicable Defaults 
(&#147;<B>Restatement
Decision Other Note Agreement Defaults</B>&#148;), having a cure period 
substantially the same as the Cure Period (the &#147;<B>Other Note Agreement 
Cure Periods</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">H. In accordance with Section&nbsp;18.1, the agreements contained 
herein require the approval of the Required Holders. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">I. Subject to the terms and provisions hereof, the 
Company has requested that the Noteholders agree to a limited waiver of the Pre-
2012
Defaults, to extend the date by which quarterly financial statements are due for
the second fiscal quarter of 2014, to extend the Cure Period and to amend 
certain terms and provisions of the Note Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B><U>AGREEMENT</U></B>:<B> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" 
ALIGN="justify"><B>NOW
THEREFORE</B> in consideration of the premises, the covenants and the agreements
herein contained and for other good and valuable consideration, the receipt and 
sufficiency of which is hereby acknowledged between the parties, the parties 
agree as
follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">The Noteholders agree to extend the Cure Period to the 
earliest of: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the earlier of: (i)&nbsp;October&nbsp;14, 2014, and 
(ii)&nbsp;the date by which the Company must under applicable Law deliver its 
quarterly
financial statements for the second fiscal quarter of 2014 (the 
&#147;<B>Extended Delivery Date</B>&#148;); </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P 
STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the earlier of (i)&nbsp;the last day of the Credit 
Agreement Cure Period or (ii)&nbsp;the Other Note Agreement Cure Periods; 
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the date that any Event of Default (other than, for 
certainty, one that results from an Applicable Default maturing into an Event of
Default)
occurs under the Note Agreement; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(d)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the date that the Company is in breach of any of its 
obligations hereunder (which for certainty shall also constitute an Event of 
Default under the
Note Agreement); </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-

ALIGN="justify">(the &#147;<B>Extended Cure Period</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">Notwithstanding anything else set forth in the Note 
Agreement or the other Financing Agreements and notwithstanding the Applicable 
Defaults, the
Noteholders waive the Pre-2012 Defaults, if any, during the Extended Cure 
Period. For certainty, subject to the deemed cure set forth in Section&nbsp;10 
of this Agreement, the foregoing waiver expires as at the end of the Extended 
Cure Period.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">The Noteholders agree that, notwithstanding 
Section&nbsp;7.1(a), the due date of the delivery of the Company&#146;s 
quarterly unaudited
consolidated financial statements for the second fiscal quarter of the 2014 
fiscal year is hereby extended from August&nbsp;29, 2014 to the earlier of: 
(a)&nbsp;the Extended Delivery Date; and (b)&nbsp;the date that such financial 
statements are due
under the Credit Agreement, including any extension thereof consented to by the 
Lenders and Agent in accordance with the Credit Agreement (the &#147;<B>Outside 
Financial Statement Delivery Date</B>&#148;). </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">The Company covenants and agrees that it will deliver 
restated financial statements for the Relevant Periods that are prepared in 
accordance with
GAAP (and otherwise in accordance with Sections 7.1(a) and (b)) to the 
Noteholders by no later than the Outside Financial Statement Delivery Date and, 
concurrently with the delivery thereof, the Company will also deliver to the 
Noteholders a
certificate of a Senior Financial Officer in accordance with Section&nbsp;7.2 
showing compliance with, and the detailed calculation of, each of the financial 
covenants set forth in Sections 10.5 and 10.6 and in the Credit Agreement, in 
each case as
at the end of each of the Company&#146;s fiscal quarters during the Relevant 
Periods. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-

<TR>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">The Company agrees that the waivers and amendments set 
forth herein are conditional upon, and will not take effect until, the Company 
pays to each
Noteholder a waiver fee equal to <B>[Redacted]</B> basis points based on 
aggregate principal amount of the Notes held by such Noteholder. 
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">The Company represents and warrants to each Noteholder 
that (a)&nbsp;to the best of its knowledge after reasonable inquiry, the Press 
Release
discloses all material information related to the Restatement Decision and it is
not aware of any omission of any material fact related thereto which renders 
such information incomplete or misleading in any material way, (b)&nbsp;it has 
not
delivered notice of a Restatement Decision Credit Agreement Default to the Agent
or any Lender or received notice of a Restatement Decision Credit Agreement 
Default from the Agent or any Lender, other than the Credit Agreement Default 
Notice,
(c)&nbsp;it has not delivered notice of a Restatement Decision Other Note 
Agreement Default to a holder of a note under the Other Note Agreements or 
received notice of a Restatement Decision Other Note Agreement Default from any 
holder of a note
under the Other Note Agreements, other than a notice equivalent to the one 
delivered to the Noteholders under the Note Agreement, (d)&nbsp;no material 
actions, suits or other litigation proceedings have been commenced against the 
Company related to
the </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>

<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P

<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">Restatement Decision, except as otherwise disclosed in 
writing by the Company to the Noteholders, and (e)&nbsp;other than Pre-2012 
Defaults, if
any, there are no other Defaults or Events of Default (other than the Specified 
Defaults) in existence as of the date hereof. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P 
STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">Without limiting the existing notice and information 
requirements in the Note Agreement, the Company covenants and agrees that it 
will provide to
each Noteholder: (a)&nbsp;a copy of any further notice of a Restatement Decision
Credit Agreement Default delivered to the Agent or any Lender under the Credit 
Agreement forthwith upon delivery thereof as well as a copy of any notices or 
other
written communications from or on behalf of the Agent or the Lenders relating to
the waiving of any Restatement Decision Credit Agreement Default, the declaring 
of a Restatement Decision Credit Agreement Default or an event of default under 
the
Credit Agreement, or the acceleration of any amounts owing under the Credit 
Agreement, and the equivalent under any Other Note Agreement, in each such case 
forthwith upon receipt thereof; (b)&nbsp;a copy of any further waiver, amendment
or consent
provided by the Agent and the Lenders in respect of the Restatement Decision 
Credit Agreement Default (a &#147;<B>Credit Agreement Waiver</B>&#148;) and the 
equivalent under any Other Note Agreement; (c)&nbsp;copies of any notices or 
written updates
provided to any Governmental Authority in connection with the Restatement 
Decision and the underlying facts related thereto, and (d)&nbsp;any further 
material information related to the Restatement Decision and the underlying 
facts related thereto
(including if a determination is made that the magnitude of the change in 
reported net income is different from what was set forth in the Press Release) 
forthwith upon the Company becoming aware thereof, provided that such 
information shall be
subject to the confidentiality provisions of Section&nbsp;21 (and not subject to
Section&nbsp;7.4). In addition, the Company covenants and agrees that it will 
not declare or make any dividend or similar Distributions to its shareholders 
until the
Applicable Defaults have been deemed to be cured under Section&nbsp;10 hereof, 
without the prior consent of the Required Holders (following which, for 
certainty, the requirements in the Note Agreement with respect to Distributions 
shall continue to
apply). </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">The Company also covenants and agrees that during the 
Extended Cure Period it will not exercise any right it may have to 
(a)&nbsp;permanently
reduce the amount of the credit facility available to it under the Credit 
Agreement from that available to it on the date hereof, as such amount is 
provided in Section&nbsp;2 of the Bank Waiver Agreement, or (b)&nbsp;repay any 
termination amounts
owing under any Hedging Agreement (as that term is defined in the Credit
Agreement), in either case without the prior written consent of the Required 
Holders. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New

Agreement Waiver is delivered to the Company in respect of the Restatement 
Decision
Credit Agreement Default and such waiver results in (a)&nbsp;any one or more of 
the Company or any Restricted Subsidiary being subject to any one or more 
restrictive conditions, covenants or terms or events of default that are not 
already provided
for in this Agreement or the Financing Agreements or (b)&nbsp;any one or more of
the Company or any Restricted Subsidiary being required to pay any additional 
consideration or waiver or similar fees in excess of the fees provided for 
herein (on a
percentage basis), then (i)&nbsp;such more restrictive conditions, covenants, 
terms or events of default shall be automatically incorporated by reference in 
this Agreement as if </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="center">- 5 - </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">set forth fully herein, <I>mutatis mutandis</I>, and no 
such provision may thereafter be waived, amended or modified under this 
Agreement, except

<TITLE>Exhibit 99.3</TITLE>

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.3 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>[EXECUTION COPY] </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>LIMITED WAIVER, AMENDMENT AND RETENTION OF RIGHTS 
</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ACKNOWLEDGMENT AGREEMENT </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>THIS AGREEMENT </B>is dated as of August&nbsp;15, 
2014 between Penn West Petroleum Ltd. (the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;) and each
noteholder (each a &#147;<B>Noteholder</B>&#148; and, collectively, the 
&#147;<B>Noteholders</B>&#148;) under the Note Purchase Agreement dated
July&nbsp;31, 2008 among the Company and the Purchasers listed in Schedule A 
attached thereto as holders
of the outstanding senior guaranteed notes of the Company issued thereunder (as 
amended, restated, supplemented or otherwise modified from time to time, the 
&#147;<B>Note Agreement</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B><U>PREAMBLE</U></B>:<B> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" 
ALIGN="justify">A. Capitalized
terms used in this Agreement without express definition shall have the same 
meanings as are ascribed to such terms in the Note Agreement and section 
references herein are to sections of the Note Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">B. The Company has issued a press release on 
July&nbsp;29, 2014 (the &#147;<B>Press Release</B>&#148;) announcing that the 
Audit Committee of
the Company&#146;s Board of Directors is conducting a voluntary internal review 
of certain of its accounting practices and that the Board of Directors of the 
Company has concluded that certain of the Company&#146;s historical financial 
statements
for the 2012 and 2013 fiscal years of the Company and the quarterly financial 
statements for its first fiscal quarter of 2014 (the &#147;<B>Relevant 
Periods</B>&#148;) must be restated (the &#147;<B>Restatement 
Decision</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">C. The Company has delivered a notice to each 
Noteholder under Section&nbsp;7.1(d) advising that as a result of the 
Restatement Decision, the
Company is in Default under: (a)&nbsp;Sections 7.1(a) and 7.1(b) (as they relate
to the statement that the financial statements be prepared in accordance with 
GAAP) (the &#147;<B>Financial Reporting Default</B>&#148;), and 
(b)&nbsp;Section&nbsp;9.6
in respect of the requirement of the Company to maintain books and records of 
account in accordance with GAAP (the &#147;<B>Covenant Default</B>&#148;, and 
together with the Financial Reporting Default, the &#147;<B>Specified 
Defaults</B>&#148;).
Under the terms of Section&nbsp;11, each Specified Default has a cure period of 
30 days after a Responsible Officer obtains actual knowledge of such default 
(the &#147;<B>Cure Period</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">D. The Company&#146;s ongoing internal review in 
connection with the Restatement Decision may include the review of financial 
statements
prepared for periods prior to the Relevant Periods (&#147;<B>Pre-Relevant Period
Financial Statements</B>&#148;) that may result in the Company becoming aware of
Defaults or Events of Default under (a)&nbsp;Sections 5.5, 7.1(a) and 7.1(b) (as
they
relate to the requirement that such Pre-Relevant Period Financial Statements be 
prepared in accordance with GAAP, and certifications to that effect in 
certificates of officers delivered pursuant to Section&nbsp;7.2), and 
(b)&nbsp;Section&nbsp;9.6 in
respect of the requirement of the Company to maintain books and records of 
account in accordance with GAAP (each, a &#147;<B>Pre-2012 Default</B>&#148; and
collectively with the Specified Defaults, the &#147;<B>Applicable 
Defaults</B>&#148;). </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="center">- 2 - </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">E. The Company is party to an amended and restated 
credit agreement dated May&nbsp;6, 2014 (the
&#147;<B>Credit Agreement</B>&#148;) between the Company, as borrower, the 
financial institutions and other persons party thereto as lenders (the 
&#147;<B>Lenders</B>&#148;) and Canadian Imperial Bank of Commerce, as agent of 
the Lenders (the
&#147;<B>Agent</B>&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">F. The accounting 
practices causing the Restatement Decision have resulted in one or more defaults
under the
Credit Agreement (each a &#147;<B>Restatement Decision Credit Agreement 
Default</B>&#148;) and each such default is subject to a cure period of 30 days 
after the giving of notice thereof by the Agent to the Company, or such later 
date as the Lenders
and the Agent may agree in accordance with the Credit Agreement (the 
&#147;<B>Credit Agreement Cure Period</B>&#148;). The Agent has provided such 
notice to the Company (the &#147;<B>Credit Agreement Default Notice</B>&#148;) 
and a copy of such
notice has been provided to each Noteholder<B><I>.</I></B> The Company, the 
Agent and the Lenders have entered into a limited waiver agreement (the 
&#147;<B>Bank Waiver Agreement</B>&#148;) in respect of the Restatement Decision
Credit Agreement
Default and a copy of the Bank Waiver Agreement has been provided to each 
Noteholder. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">G. The Company is a party to six 
other Note
Agreements (the &#147;<B>Other Note Agreements</B>&#148;) having terms 
substantially the same as the Note Agreement, and there exists, under each one, 
defaults that are substantially equivalent to the Applicable Defaults 
(&#147;<B>Restatement
Decision Other Note Agreement Defaults</B>&#148;), having a cure period 
substantially the same as the Cure Period (the &#147;<B>Other Note Agreement 
Cure Periods</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">H. In accordance with Section&nbsp;18.1, the 
agreements contained herein require the approval of the Required Holders. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">I. Subject to the terms and provisions hereof, the 
Company has requested that the Noteholders agree to a limited waiver of the Pre-
2012
Defaults, to extend the date by which quarterly financial statements are due for
the second fiscal quarter of 2014, to extend the Cure Period and to amend 
certain terms and provisions of the Note Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B><U>AGREEMENT</U></B>:<B> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" 
ALIGN="justify"><B>NOW
THEREFORE</B> in consideration of the premises, the covenants and the agreements
herein contained and for other good and valuable consideration, the receipt and 
sufficiency of which is hereby acknowledged between the parties, the parties 
agree as
follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">The Noteholders agree to extend the Cure Period to the 
earliest of: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the earlier of: (i)&nbsp;October&nbsp;14, 2014, and 
(ii)&nbsp;the date by which the Company must under applicable Law deliver its 
quarterly
financial statements for the second fiscal quarter of 2014 (the 
&#147;<B>Extended Delivery Date</B>&#148;); </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P 
STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the earlier of (i)&nbsp;the last day of the Credit 
Agreement Cure Period or (ii)&nbsp;the Other Note Agreement Cure Periods; 
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(c)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the date that any Event of Default (other than, for 
certainty, one that results from an Applicable Default maturing into an Event of
Default)
occurs under the Note Agreement; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="center">- 3 - </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(d)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the date that the Company is in breach of any of its 
obligations hereunder (which for certainty shall also constitute an Event of 
Default under the
Note Agreement); </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" 
ALIGN="justify">(the &#147;<B>Extended Cure Period</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">Notwithstanding anything else set forth in the Note 
Agreement or the other Financing Agreements and notwithstanding the Applicable 
Defaults, the
Noteholders waive the Pre-2012 Defaults, if any, during the Extended Cure 
Period. For certainty, subject to the deemed cure set forth in Section&nbsp;10 
of this Agreement, the foregoing waiver expires as at the end of the Extended
Cure Period.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">The Noteholders agree that, notwithstanding Section 
7.1(a), the due date of the delivery of the Company&#146;s quarterly unaudited 
consolidated
financial statements for the second fiscal quarter of the 2014 fiscal year is 
hereby extended from August 29, 2014 to the earlier of: (a) the Extended 
Delivery Date; and (b) the date that such financial statements are due under the
Credit Agreement,
including any extension thereof consented to by the Lenders and Agent in 
accordance with the Credit Agreement (the &#147;<B>Outside Financial Statement 
Delivery Date</B>&#148;). </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">The Company covenants and agrees that it will deliver 
restated financial statements for the Relevant Periods that are prepared in 
accordance with
GAAP (and otherwise in accordance with Sections 7.1(a) and (b)) to the 
Noteholders by no later than the Outside Financial Statement Delivery Date and, 
concurrently with the delivery thereof, the Company will also deliver to the 
Noteholders a
certificate of a Senior Financial Officer in accordance with Section&nbsp;7.2 
showing compliance with, and the detailed calculation of, each of the financial 
covenants set forth in Sections 10.5 and 10.6 and in the Credit Agreement, in 
each case as
at the end of each of the Company&#146;s fiscal quarters during the Relevant 
Periods. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5.</TD>

<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>Exhibit 99.4</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.4 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>[EXECUTION COPY] </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>LIMITED WAIVER, AMENDMENT AND RETENTION OF RIGHTS 
</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ACKNOWLEDGMENT AGREEMENT </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>THIS AGREEMENT </B>is dated as of August&nbsp;15, 
2014 between Penn West Petroleum Ltd. (the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;) and each
noteholder (each a &#147;<B>Noteholder</B>&#148; and, collectively, the 
&#147;<B>Noteholders</B>&#148;) under the Note Purchase Agreement dated 
May&nbsp;5, 2009 among the Company and the Purchasers listed in Schedule A 
attached thereto as holders of
the outstanding senior guaranteed notes of the Company issued thereunder (as 
amended, restated, supplemented or otherwise modified from time to time, the 
&#147;<B>Note Agreement</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><U><B>PREAMBLE</B></U>: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">A. 
Capitalized terms
used in this Agreement without express definition shall have the same meanings 
as are ascribed to such terms in the Note Agreement and section references 
herein are to sections of the Note Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">B. The Company has issued a press release on 
July&nbsp;29, 2014 (the &#147;<B>Press Release</B>&#148;) announcing that the 
Audit Committee of
the Company&#146;s Board of Directors is conducting a voluntary internal review 
of certain of its accounting practices and that the Board of Directors of the 
Company has concluded that certain of the Company&#146;s historical financial 
statements
for the 2012 and 2013 fiscal years of the Company and the quarterly financial 
statements for its first fiscal quarter of 2014 (the &#147;<B>Relevant 
Periods</B>&#148;) must be restated (the &#147;<B>Restatement 
Decision</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">C. The Company has delivered a notice to each 
Noteholder under Section&nbsp;7.1(d) advising that as a result of the 
Restatement Decision, the
Company is in Default under: (a)&nbsp;Sections 7.1(a) and 7.1(b) (as they relate
to the statement that the financial statements be prepared in accordance with 
GAAP) (the &#147;<B>Financial Reporting Default</B>&#148;), and 
(b)&nbsp;Section&nbsp;9.6
in respect of the requirement of the Company to maintain books and records of 
account in accordance with GAAP (the &#147;<B>Covenant Default</B>&#148;, and 
together with the Financial Reporting Default, the &#147;<B>Specified 
Defaults</B>&#148;).
Under the terms of Section&nbsp;11, each Specified Default has a cure period of 
30 days after a Responsible Officer obtains actual knowledge of such default 
(the &#147;<B>Cure Period</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">D. The Company&#146;s ongoing internal review in 
connection with the Restatement Decision may include the review of financial 
statements
prepared for periods prior to the Relevant Periods (&#147;<B>Pre-Relevant Period
Financial Statements</B>&#148;) that may result in the Company becoming aware of
Defaults or Events of Default under (a)&nbsp;Sections 5.5, 7.1(a) and 7.1(b) (as
they
relate to the requirement that such Pre-Relevant Period Financial Statements be 
prepared in accordance with GAAP, and certifications to that effect in 
certificates of officers delivered pursuant to Section&nbsp;7.2), and 
(b)&nbsp;Section&nbsp;9.6 in
respect of the requirement of the Company to maintain books and records of 
account in accordance with GAAP (each, a &#147;<B>Pre-2012 Default</B>&#148; and
collectively with the Specified Defaults, the &#147;<B>Applicable 
Defaults</B>&#148;). </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="center">- 2 - </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">E. The Company is party to an amended and restated 
credit agreement dated May&nbsp;6, 2014 (the
&#147;<B>Credit Agreement</B>&#148;) between the Company, as borrower, the 
financial institutions and other persons party thereto as lenders (the 
&#147;<B>Lenders</B>&#148;) and Canadian Imperial Bank of Commerce, as agent of 
the Lenders (the
&#147;<B>Agent</B>&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">F. The accounting 
practices causing the Restatement Decision have resulted in one or more defaults
under the
Credit Agreement (each a &#147;<B>Restatement Decision Credit Agreement 
Default</B>&#148;) and each such default is subject to a cure period of 30 days 
after the giving of notice thereof by the Agent to the Company, or such later 
date as the Lenders
and the Agent may agree in accordance with the Credit Agreement (the 
&#147;<B>Credit Agreement Cure Period</B>&#148;). The Agent has provided such 
notice to the Company (the &#147;<B>Credit Agreement Default Notice</B>&#148;) 
and a copy of such
notice has been provided to each Noteholder<B><I>.</I></B> The Company, the 
Agent and the Lenders have entered into a limited waiver agreement (the 
&#147;<B>Bank Waiver Agreement</B>&#148;) in respect of the Restatement Decision
Credit Agreement
Default and a copy of the Bank Waiver Agreement has been provided to each 
Noteholder. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">G. The Company is a party to six 
other Note
Agreements (the &#147;<B>Other Note Agreements</B>&#148;) having terms 
substantially the same as the Note Agreement, and there exists, under each one, 
defaults that are substantially equivalent to the Applicable Defaults 
(&#147;<B>Restatement
Decision Other Note Agreement Defaults</B>&#148;), having a cure period 
substantially the same as the Cure Period (the &#147;<B>Other Note Agreement 
Cure Periods</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">H. In accordance with Section&nbsp;18.1, the
agreements contained herein require the approval of the Required Holders. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">I. Subject to the terms and provisions hereof, the 
Company has requested that the Noteholders agree to a limited waiver of the Pre-
2012
Defaults, to extend the date by which quarterly financial statements are due for
the second fiscal quarter of 2014, to extend the Cure Period and to amend 
certain terms and provisions of the Note Agreement. </P>

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.5 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>[EXECUTION COPY] </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>LIMITED WAIVER, AMENDMENT AND RETENTION OF RIGHTS 
</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ACKNOWLEDGMENT AGREEMENT </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>THIS AGREEMENT </B>is dated as of August&nbsp;15, 
2014 between Penn West Petroleum Ltd. (the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;) and each
noteholder (each a &#147;<B>Noteholder</B>&#148; and, collectively, the 
&#147;<B>Noteholders</B>&#148;) under the Note Purchase Agreement dated 
March&nbsp;16, 2010 among the Company and the Purchasers listed in Schedule A 
attached thereto as holders
of the outstanding senior guaranteed notes of the Company issued thereunder (as 
amended, restated, supplemented or otherwise modified from time to time, the 
&#147;<B>Note Agreement</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B><U>PREAMBLE</U></B>:<B> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" 
ALIGN="justify">A. Capitalized
terms used in this Agreement without express definition shall have the same 
meanings as are ascribed to such terms in the Note Agreement and section 
references herein are to sections of the Note Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">B. The Company has issued a press release on 
July&nbsp;29, 2014 (the &#147;<B>Press Release</B>&#148;) announcing that the 
Audit Committee of
the Company&#146;s Board of Directors is conducting a voluntary internal review 
of certain of its accounting practices and that the Board of Directors of the 
Company has concluded that certain of the Company&#146;s historical financial 
statements
for the 2012 and 2013 fiscal years of the Company and the quarterly financial 
statements for its first fiscal quarter of 2014 (the &#147;<B>Relevant 
Periods</B>&#148;) must be restated (the &#147;<B>Restatement 
Decision</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">C. The Company has delivered a notice to each 
Noteholder under Section&nbsp;7.1(d) advising that as a result of the 
Restatement Decision, the
Company is in Default under: (a)&nbsp;Sections 7.1(a) and 7.1(b) (as they relate
to the statement that the financial statements be prepared in accordance with 
GAAP) (the &#147;<B>Financial Reporting Default</B>&#148;), and 
(b)&nbsp;Section&nbsp;9.6
in respect of the requirement of the Company to maintain books and records of 
account in accordance with GAAP (the &#147;<B>Covenant Default</B>&#148;, and 
together with the Financial Reporting Default, the &#147;<B>Specified 
Defaults</B>&#148;).
Under the terms of Section&nbsp;11, each Specified Default has a cure period of 
30 days after a Responsible Officer obtains actual knowledge of such default 
(the &#147;<B>Cure Period</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">D. The Company&#146;s ongoing internal review in 
connection with the Restatement Decision may include the review of financial 
statements
prepared for periods prior to the Relevant Periods (&#147;<B>Pre-Relevant Period
Financial Statements</B>&#148;) that may result in the Company becoming aware of
Defaults or Events of Default under (a)&nbsp;Sections 5.5, 7.1(a) and 7.1(b) (as
they
relate to the requirement that such Pre-Relevant Period Financial Statements be 
prepared in accordance with GAAP, and certifications to that effect in 
certificates of officers delivered pursuant to Section&nbsp;7.2), and 
(b)&nbsp;Section&nbsp;9.6 in
respect of the requirement of the Company to maintain books and records of 
account in accordance with GAAP (each, a &#147;<B>Pre-2012 Default</B>&#148; and
collectively with the Specified Defaults, the &#147;<B>Applicable 
Defaults</B>&#148;). </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="center">- 2 - </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">E. The Company is party to an amended and restated 
credit agreement dated May&nbsp;6, 2014 (the
&#147;<B>Credit Agreement</B>&#148;) between the Company, as borrower, the 
financial institutions and other persons party thereto as lenders (the 
&#147;<B>Lenders</B>&#148;) and Canadian Imperial Bank of Commerce, as agent of 
the Lenders (the
&#147;<B>Agent</B>&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">F. The accounting 
practices causing the Restatement Decision have resulted in one or more defaults
under the
Credit Agreement (each a &#147;<B>Restatement Decision Credit Agreement 
Default</B>&#148;) and each such default is subject to a cure period of 30 days 
after the giving of notice thereof by the Agent to the Company, or such later 
date as the Lenders
and the Agent may agree in accordance with the Credit Agreement (the 
&#147;<B>Credit Agreement Cure Period</B>&#148;). The Agent has provided such 
notice to the Company (the &#147;<B>Credit Agreement Default Notice</B>&#148;) 
and a copy of such
notice has been provided to each Noteholder<B><I>.</I></B> The Company, the 
Agent and the Lenders have entered into a limited waiver agreement (the 
&#147;<B>Bank Waiver Agreement</B>&#148;) in respect of the Restatement Decision
Credit Agreement
Default and a copy of the Bank Waiver Agreement has been provided to each 
Noteholder. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">G. The Company is a party to six 
other Note
Agreements (the &#147;<B>Other Note Agreements</B>&#148;) having terms 
substantially the same as the Note Agreement, and there exists, under each one, 
defaults that are substantially equivalent to the Applicable Defaults 
(&#147;<B>Restatement
Decision Other Note Agreement Defaults</B>&#148;), having a cure period 
substantially the same as the Cure Period (the &#147;<B>Other Note Agreement 
Cure Periods</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">H. In accordance with Section&nbsp;18.1, the 
agreements contained herein require the approval of the Required Holders. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">I. Subject to the terms and provisions hereof, the
Company has requested that the Noteholders agree to a limited waiver of the Pre-
2012
Defaults, to extend the date by which quarterly financial statements are due for
the second fiscal quarter of 2014, to extend the Cure Period and to amend 
certain terms and provisions of the Note Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B><U>AGREEMENT</U></B>:<B> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" 
ALIGN="justify"><B>NOW
THEREFORE</B> in consideration of the premises, the covenants and the agreements
herein contained and for other good and valuable consideration, the receipt and 
sufficiency of which is hereby acknowledged between the parties, the parties 
agree as
follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

at the end of each of the Company&#146;s fiscal quarters during the Relevant

Release
discloses all material information related to the Restatement Decision and it is

not

(c)&nbsp;it has not delivered notice of a Restatement Decision Other Note

the </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

will provide to
each Noteholder: (a)&nbsp;a copy of any further notice of a Restatement Decision
Credit Agreement Default delivered to the Agent or any Lender under the Credit

or consent

provided to any Governmental Authority in connection with the Restatement

facts related thereto
(including if a determination is made that the magnitude of the change in 
reported net income is different from what was set forth in the Press Release) 
forthwith upon the Company becoming aware thereof, provided that such 
information shall be
subject to the confidentiality provisions of Section&nbsp;21 (and not subject to
Section&nbsp;7.4). In addition, the Company covenants and agrees that it will 
not declare or make any dividend or similar Distributions to its shareholders 
until the
Applicable Defaults have been deemed to be cured under Section&nbsp;10 hereof, 
without the prior consent of the Required Holders (following which, for 
certainty, the requirements in the Note Agreement with respect to Distributions 
shall continue to
apply). </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-

owing under any Hedging Agreement (as that term is defined in the Credit

<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">set forth fully herein, <I>mutatis mutandis</I>, and no 
such provision may thereafter be waived, amended or modified under this 
Agreement, except
in accordance with the provisions of the Note Agreement, and/or (ii)&nbsp;such 
additional consideration or waiver or similar fees shall be payable to each 
Noteholder; provided, for greater certainty, this Clause 9 shall not apply in 
any manner in
regards to the Bank Waiver Agreement as currently in place and the terms and 
conditions included therein, and shall not limit or affect the existing 
provisions of the Note Agreement. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>Exhibit 99.6</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.6 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>[EXECUTION COPY] </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>LIMITED WAIVER, AMENDMENT AND RETENTION OF RIGHTS 
</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ACKNOWLEDGMENT AGREEMENT </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>THIS AGREEMENT </B>is dated as of August&nbsp;15, 
2014 between Penn West Petroleum Ltd. (the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;) and each
noteholder (each a &#147;<B>Noteholder</B>&#148; and, collectively, the 
&#147;<B>Noteholders</B>&#148;) under the Note Purchase Agreement dated 
December&nbsp;2, 2010 among the Company and the Purchasers listed in Schedule A 
attached thereto as
holders of the outstanding senior guaranteed notes of the Company issued 
thereunder (as amended, restated, supplemented or otherwise modified from time 
to time, the &#147;<B>Note Agreement</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B><U>PREAMBLE</U></B>:<B> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" 
ALIGN="justify">A. Capitalized
terms used in this Agreement without express definition shall have the same 
meanings as are ascribed to such terms in the Note Agreement and section 
references herein are to sections of the Note Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">B. The Company has issued a press release on 
July&nbsp;29, 2014 (the &#147;<B>Press Release</B>&#148;) announcing that the 
Audit Committee of
the Company&#146;s Board of Directors is conducting a voluntary internal review 
of certain of its accounting practices and that the Board of Directors of the 
Company has concluded that certain of the Company&#146;s historical financial 
statements
for the 2012 and 2013 fiscal years of the Company and the quarterly financial 
statements for its first fiscal quarter of 2014 (the &#147;<B>Relevant 
Periods</B>&#148;) must be restated (the &#147;<B>Restatement 
Decision</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">C. The Company has delivered a notice to each 
Noteholder under Section&nbsp;7.1(d) advising that as a result of the 
Restatement Decision, the
Company is in Default under: (a)&nbsp;Sections 7.1(a) and 7.1(b) (as they relate
to the statement that the financial statements be prepared in accordance with 
GAAP) (the &#147;<B>Financial Reporting Default</B>&#148;), and 
(b)&nbsp;Section&nbsp;9.6
in respect of the requirement of the Company to maintain books and records of 
account in accordance with GAAP (the &#147;<B>Covenant Default</B>&#148;, and
together with the Financial Reporting Default, the &#147;<B>Specified 
Defaults</B>&#148;).
Under the terms of Section&nbsp;11, each Specified Default has a cure period of 
30 days after a Responsible Officer obtains actual knowledge of such default 
(the &#147;<B>Cure Period</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">D. The Company&#146;s ongoing internal review in 
connection with the Restatement Decision may include the review of financial 
statements
prepared for periods prior to the Relevant Periods (&#147;<B>Pre-Relevant Period
Financial Statements</B>&#148;) that may result in the Company becoming aware of
Defaults or Events of Default under (a)&nbsp;Sections 5.1(e), 5.2(e), 7.1(a) and
7.1(b)
(as they relate to the requirement that such Pre-Relevant Period Financial 
Statements be prepared in accordance with GAAP, and certifications to that 
effect in certificates of officers delivered pursuant to Section&nbsp;7.2), and
(b)&nbsp;Section&nbsp;9.6 in respect of the requirement of the Company to 
maintain books and records of account in accordance with GAAP (each, a 
&#147;<B>Pre-2012 Default</B>&#148; and collectively with the Specified 
Defaults, the
&#147;<B>Applicable Defaults</B>&#148;). </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="center">- 2 - </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">E. The Company is party to an amended and restated 
credit agreement dated May&nbsp;6, 2014 (the
&#147;<B>Credit Agreement</B>&#148;) between the Company, as borrower, the 
financial institutions and other persons party thereto as lenders (the 
&#147;<B>Lenders</B>&#148;) and Canadian Imperial Bank of Commerce, as agent of 
the Lenders (the
&#147;<B>Agent</B>&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">F. The accounting 
practices causing the Restatement Decision have resulted in one or more defaults
under the
Credit Agreement (each a &#147;<B>Restatement Decision Credit Agreement 
Default</B>&#148;) and each such default is subject to a cure period of 30 days 
after the giving of notice thereof by the Agent to the Company, or such later 
date as the Lenders
and the Agent may agree in accordance with the Credit Agreement (the 
&#147;<B>Credit Agreement Cure Period</B>&#148;). The Agent has provided such 
notice to the Company (the &#147;<B>Credit Agreement Default Notice</B>&#148;) 
and a copy of such
notice has been provided to each Noteholder<B><I>.</I></B> The Company, the 
Agent and the Lenders have entered into a limited waiver agreement (the 
&#147;<B>Bank Waiver Agreement</B>&#148;) in respect of the Restatement Decision
Credit Agreement
Default and a copy of the Bank Waiver Agreement has been provided to each 
Noteholder. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">G. The Company is a party to six 
other Note
Agreements (the &#147;<B>Other Note Agreements</B>&#148;) having terms 
substantially the same as the Note Agreement, and there exists, under each one, 
defaults that are substantially equivalent to the Applicable Defaults 
(&#147;<B>Restatement
Decision Other Note Agreement Defaults</B>&#148;), having a cure period 
substantially the same as the Cure Period (the &#147;<B>Other Note Agreement 
Cure Periods</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">H. In accordance with Section&nbsp;18.1, the agreements contained 
herein require the approval of the Required Holders. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">I. Subject to the terms and provisions hereof, the 
Company has requested that the Noteholders agree to a limited waiver of the Pre-
2012
Defaults, to extend the date by which quarterly financial statements are due for
the second fiscal quarter of 2014, to extend the Cure Period and to amend 
certain terms and provisions of the Note Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B><U>AGREEMENT</U></B>:<B> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" 
ALIGN="justify"><B>NOW
THEREFORE</B> in consideration of the premises, the covenants and the agreements
herein contained and for other good and valuable consideration, the receipt and 
sufficiency of which is hereby acknowledged between the parties, the parties 
agree as
follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">The Noteholders agree to extend the Cure Period to the 
earliest of: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the earlier of: (i)&nbsp;October&nbsp;14, 2014, and 
(ii)&nbsp;the date by which the Company must under applicable Law deliver its 
quarterly
financial statements for the second fiscal quarter of 2014 (the 
&#147;<B>Extended Delivery Date</B>&#148;); </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P 
STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the earlier of (i)&nbsp;the last day of the Credit 
Agreement Cure Period or (ii)&nbsp;the Other Note Agreement Cure Periods; 
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(c)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the date that any Event of Default (other than, for 
certainty, one that results from an Applicable Default maturing into an Event of
Default)
occurs under the Note Agreement; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="center">- 3 - </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(d)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the date that the Company is in breach of any of its 
obligations hereunder (which for certainty shall also constitute an Event of 
Default under the
Note Agreement); </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" 
ALIGN="justify">(the &#147;<B>Extended Cure Period</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">Notwithstanding anything else set forth in the Note 
Agreement or the other Financing Agreements and notwithstanding the Applicable 
Defaults, the
Noteholders waive the Pre-2012 Defaults, if any, during the Extended Cure 
Period. For certainty, subject to the deemed cure set forth in Section&nbsp;10 
of this Agreement, the foregoing waiver expires as at the end of the Extended 
Cure Period.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">The Noteholders agree that, notwithstanding 
Section&nbsp;7.1(a), the due date of the delivery of the Company&#146;s 
quarterly unaudited
consolidated financial statements for the second fiscal quarter of the 2014 
fiscal year is hereby extended from August&nbsp;29, 2014 to the earlier of: 
(a)&nbsp;the Extended Delivery Date; and (b)&nbsp;the date that such financial 
statements are due
under the Credit Agreement, including any extension thereof consented to by the 
Lenders and Agent in accordance with the Credit Agreement (the &#147;<B>Outside 
Financial Statement Delivery Date</B>&#148;). </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">The Company covenants and agrees that it will deliver 
restated financial statements for the Relevant Periods that are prepared in 
accordance with
GAAP (and otherwise in accordance with Sections 7.1(a) and (b)) to the 
Noteholders by no later than the Outside Financial Statement Delivery Date and, 
concurrently with the delivery thereof, the Company will also deliver to the 
Noteholders a
certificate of a Senior Financial Officer in accordance with Section&nbsp;7.2 
showing compliance with, and the detailed calculation of, each of the financial
