<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>Exhibit 99.7</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.7 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>[EXECUTION COPY] </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>LIMITED WAIVER, AMENDMENT AND RETENTION OF RIGHTS 
</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ACKNOWLEDGMENT AGREEMENT </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>THIS AGREEMENT </B>is dated as of August&nbsp;15, 
2014 between Penn West Petroleum Ltd. (the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;) and each
noteholder (each a &#147;<B>Noteholder</B>&#148; and, collectively, the 
&#147;<B>Noteholders</B>&#148;) under the Note Purchase Agreement dated 
November&nbsp;30, 2011 among the Company and the Purchasers listed in Schedule A
attached thereto as
holders of the outstanding senior guaranteed notes of the Company issued 
thereunder (as amended, restated, supplemented or otherwise modified from time 
to time, the &#147;<B>Note Agreement</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B><U>PREAMBLE</U></B>:<B> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" 
ALIGN="justify">A. Capitalized
terms used in this Agreement without express definition shall have the same 
meanings as are ascribed to such terms in the Note Agreement and section 
references herein are to sections of the Note Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">B. The Company has issued a press release on 
July&nbsp;29, 2014 (the &#147;<B>Press Release</B>&#148;) announcing that the 
Audit Committee of
the Company&#146;s Board of Directors is conducting a voluntary internal review 
of certain of its accounting practices and that the Board of Directors of the 
Company has concluded that certain of the Company&#146;s historical financial 
statements
for the 2012 and 2013 fiscal years of the Company and the quarterly financial 
statements for its first fiscal quarter of 2014 (the &#147;<B>Relevant 
Periods</B>&#148;) must be restated (the &#147;<B>Restatement 
Decision</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">C. The Company has delivered a notice to each 
Noteholder under Section&nbsp;7.1(d) advising that as a result of the 
Restatement Decision, the
Company is in Default under: (a)&nbsp;Sections 7.1(a) and 7.1(b) (as they relate
to the statement that the financial statements be prepared in accordance with 
GAAP) (the &#147;<B>Financial Reporting Default</B>&#148;), and 
(b)&nbsp;Section&nbsp;9.6
in respect of the requirement of the Company to maintain books and records of 
account in accordance with GAAP (the &#147;<B>Covenant Default</B>&#148;, and 
together with the Financial Reporting Default, the &#147;<B>Specified 
Defaults</B>&#148;).
Under the terms of Section&nbsp;11, each Specified Default has a cure period of 
30 days after a Responsible Officer obtains actual knowledge of such default 
(the &#147;<B>Cure Period</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">D. The Company&#146;s ongoing internal review in 
connection with the Restatement Decision may include the review of financial 
statements
prepared for periods prior to the Relevant Periods (&#147;<B>Pre-Relevant Period
Financial Statements</B>&#148;) that may result in the Company becoming aware of
Defaults or Events of Default under (a)&nbsp;Sections 5.5, 7.1(a) and 7.1(b) (as
they
relate to the requirement that such Pre-Relevant Period Financial Statements be 
prepared in accordance with GAAP, and certifications to that effect in 
certificates of officers delivered pursuant to Section&nbsp;7.2), and 
(b)&nbsp;Section&nbsp;9.6 in
respect of the requirement of the Company to maintain books and records of 
account in accordance with GAAP (each, a &#147;<B>Pre-2012 Default</B>&#148; and
collectively with the Specified Defaults, the &#147;<B>Applicable 
Defaults</B>&#148;). </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="center">- 2 - </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">E. The Company is party to an amended and restated 
credit agreement dated May&nbsp;6, 2014 (the
&#147;<B>Credit Agreement</B>&#148;) between the Company, as borrower, the 
financial institutions and other persons party thereto as lenders (the 
&#147;<B>Lenders</B>&#148;) and Canadian Imperial Bank of Commerce, as agent of 
the Lenders (the
&#147;<B>Agent</B>&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">F. The accounting 
practices causing the Restatement Decision have resulted in one or more defaults
under the
Credit Agreement (each a &#147;<B>Restatement Decision Credit Agreement 
Default</B>&#148;) and each such default is subject to a cure period of 30 days 
after the giving of notice thereof by the Agent to the Company, or such later 
date as the Lenders
and the Agent may agree in accordance with the Credit Agreement (the 
&#147;<B>Credit Agreement Cure Period</B>&#148;). The Agent has provided such 
notice to the Company (the &#147;<B>Credit Agreement Default Notice</B>&#148;) 
and a copy of such
notice has been provided to each Noteholder<B><I>.</I></B> The Company, the 
Agent and the Lenders have entered into a limited waiver agreement (the 
&#147;<B>Bank Waiver Agreement</B>&#148;) in respect of the Restatement Decision
Credit Agreement
Default and a copy of the Bank Waiver Agreement has been provided to each 
Noteholder. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt;
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">G. The Company is a party to six 
other Note
Agreements (the &#147;<B>Other Note Agreements</B>&#148;) having terms 
substantially the same as the Note Agreement, and there exists, under each one, 
defaults that are substantially equivalent to the Applicable Defaults 
(&#147;<B>Restatement
Decision Other Note Agreement Defaults</B>&#148;), having a cure period 
substantially the same as the Cure Period (the &#147;<B>Other Note Agreement 
Cure Periods</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">H. In accordance with Section&nbsp;18.1, the agreements contained 
herein require the approval of the Required Holders. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">I. Subject to the terms and provisions hereof, the 
Company has requested that the Noteholders agree to a limited waiver of the Pre-
2012
Defaults, to extend the date by which quarterly financial statements are due for
the second fiscal quarter of 2014, to extend the Cure Period and to amend 
certain terms and provisions of the Note Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B><U>AGREEMENT</U></B>:<B> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" 
ALIGN="justify"><B>NOW
THEREFORE</B> in consideration of the premises, the covenants and the agreements
herein contained and for other good and valuable consideration, the receipt and 
sufficiency of which is hereby acknowledged between the parties, the parties 
agree as
follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">The Noteholders agree to extend the Cure Period to the 
earliest of: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the earlier of: (i)&nbsp;October&nbsp;14, 2014, and 
(ii)&nbsp;the date by which the Company must under applicable Law deliver its 
quarterly
financial statements for the second fiscal quarter of 2014 (the 
&#147;<B>Extended Delivery Date</B>&#148;); </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P 
STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the earlier of (i)&nbsp;the last day of the Credit 
Agreement Cure Period or (ii)&nbsp;the Other Note Agreement Cure Periods; 
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(c)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">the date that any Event of Default (other than, for 
certainty, one that results from an Applicable Default maturing into an Event of
Default)
occurs under the Note Agreement; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="center">- 3 - </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(d)</TD>

<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>Exhibit 99.8</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.8 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>AMENDED AND RESTATED LIMITED WAIVER AND RETENTION 
OF RIGHTS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ACKNOWLEDGMENT AGREEMENT </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>THIS AGREEMENT</B> is dated as of August&nbsp;12, 
2014 between Penn West Petroleum Ltd. and Canadian Imperial Bank of Commerce, as
Agent on
behalf of the Lenders.<B> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>PREAMBLE</U></B>:<B> </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">A. Reference is made to the amended and restated 
credit agreement dated May 6, 2014 (the &#147;<B>Credit Agreement</B>&#148;) 
between Penn
West Petroleum Ltd. (the &#147;<B>Borrower</B>&#148;), the financial 
institutions and other persons party thereto as lenders (the 
&#147;<B>Lenders</B>&#148;) and Canadian Imperial Bank of Commerce, as agent of 
the Lenders (the
&#147;<B>Agent</B>&#148;). Capitalized terms used in this Agreement without 
express definition shall have the same meanings as are ascribed to such terms in
the Credit Agreement and section references herein are to sections of the Credit
Agreement.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-
family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">B. The Borrower has issued a press 
release on July&nbsp;29, 2014 (the &#147;<B>Press Release</B>&#148;) announcing 
that the Audit
Committee of the Borrower&#146;s Board of Directors is conducting a voluntary 
internal review of certain of its accounting practices and that the Board of 
Directors of the Borrower has concluded that the Borrower&#146;s financial 
statements for the
2012 and 2013 fiscal years of the Borrower and the quarterly financial
statements for its first fiscal quarter of 2014 (the &#147;<B>Relevant 
Periods</B>&#148;) must be restated (the &#147;<B>Restatement 
Decision</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">C. The Borrower has delivered a notice to the Agent 
under Section 14.1(c) advising that as a result of the Restatement Decision, the
Borrower
is in Default under: (a) Section 13.1(i) (as it relates to the statement that 
the financial statements were prepared in accordance with GAAP) (the 
&#147;<B>Representation Default</B>&#148;), and (b) Section 14.1(j) in respect 
of the requirement of
the Borrower to maintain books and records of account in accordance with GAAP 
(the &#147;the &#147;<B>Covenant Default</B>&#148;, and together with the 
Representation Default, the &#147;<B>Specified Defaults</B>&#148;). Under the 
terms of Section
18.1, each Specified Default has a cure period of 30 days after notice thereof 
has been given by the Agent to the Borrower (the &#147;<B>Cure 
Period</B>&#148;). The Agent has provided such notice to the Borrower. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">D. The Borrower has approximately $2.1 billion of 
unsecured notes (the &#147;<B>Notes</B>&#148;) outstanding to various 
noteholders
(collectively, the &#147;<B>Noteholders</B>&#148;) pursuant to seven separate 
note purchase agreements (collectively, the &#147;<B>Note Purchase 
Agreements</B>&#148;), the latest of which was entered into in November 2011. 
</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">E. The Restatement Decision has resulted in one or 
more defaults under one or more of the Note Purchase Agreements (each a
&#147;<B>Restatement Decision Note Default</B>&#148;) and each such default is 
subject to a cure period of 30 days after the giving of notice thereof, or such 
later date as the Noteholders may agree in accordance with the applicable Note 
Purchase
Agreements (the &#147;<B>Note Cure Period</B>&#148;) and notices of such 
Restatement Decision Note Defaults have been issued to the Noteholders as 
required under the applicable Note Purchase Agreements (the &#147;<B>Note 
Default Notices</B>&#148;)
and copies of such notices have been provided to the Agent. </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="center">- 2 - </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">F. As a result of the Specified Defaults, under the 
terms of the Credit Agreement the Borrower is
unable to make any further Drawdowns while the Specified Defaults are continuing
but the Borrower has an immediate need to borrow funds under the Credit 
Agreement in order to satisfy certain immediate accounts payable and related 
obligations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">G. In accordance with Section&nbsp;21.16(b), the 
waiver of the Specified Defaults for the purposes set forth herein requires the 
approval of
the Majority Lenders. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-
size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">H. On July 31, 2014, the
Agent on behalf of the Majority Lenders and the Borrower entered into a Limited 
Waiver and
Retention of Rights Acknowledgment Agreement (the &#147;<B>July Waiver 
Agreement</B>&#148;) wherein certain Drawdowns up to $100,000,000 by way of
Swing Line Loans and overdraft borrowing, Rollovers or replacement of then 
existing Bankers&#146;
Acceptances and extensions of Swing Line Letters of Credit were permitted during
the Cure Period. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-
size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">I. As of the date 
hereof, the
outstanding Advances under Tranche A and Tranche B (other than Swing Line Loans)
are as set forth in Schedule A hereto (the &#147;<B>Existing Syndicated 
Advances</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify">J. Subject to the terms and provisions hereof, the 
Borrower has requested that the Lenders continue to waive, and the Majority 
Lenders have
determined to continue to waive, the Specified Defaults for the limited purposes
set out herein, to extend the date by which quarterly financial statements are 
due for the second fiscal quarter of 2014 and to extend the Cure Period subject 
to the
terms and provisions set forth herein. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman"><B><U>AGREEMENT</U></B>:<B> </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>NOW THEREFORE</B> in consideration of the 
premises, the covenants and the agreements herein contained and for other good 
and valuable
consideration, the receipt and sufficiency of which is hereby acknowledged 
between the Parties, the Parties agree as follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-
size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman; font-size:12pt">The Lenders agree to extend the Cure Period to the 
earliest of: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
